            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

</p><p><b>Denjiro</b> is a <a href="/wiki/Samurai" title="Samurai">samurai</a> from <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a> and one of the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a> who served as <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>'s retainers.<sup id="cite_ref-c939_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c939-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> He currently serves as the <a href="/wiki/Daimyo" title="Daimyo">daimyo</a> of <a href="/wiki/Kibi" class="mw-redirect" title="Kibi">Kibi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1120_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1120-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After becoming grief-stricken over Oden's execution 20 years ago, Denjiro's facial structure changed, and he started going under the name <b>Kyoshiro</b>. With this new identity, he became a <a href="/wiki/Yakuza" title="Yakuza">yakuza</a> boss and recruited followers to form the <a href="/wiki/Kyoshiro_Family" title="Kyoshiro Family">Kyoshiro Family</a>. Eventually, he started working for Oden's usurper, shogun <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a>, as his money changer and bodyguard; he would successfully keep his true allegiance to the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a> a secret and bide his time until the Scabbards finally reunited to take down Orochi and <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c975_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c975-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Apart from his Kyoshiro identity, Denjiro would disguise himself at night to rob the wealthy <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Flower Capital</a> citizens and give to the poor residents of <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital#Ebisu_Town" title="Flower Capital">Ebisu Town</a>, earning him the moniker <b>"Ushimitsu Kozo"</b>. He also took care of Oden's daughter <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Kouzuki Hiyori</a> for the past 13 years, raising her to become the oiran Komurasaki.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Denjiro is a very tall and muscular man, standing at 306&#160;cm.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs96_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs96-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Before Oden's execution, he used to have rather big and round eyes as well as dark blue hair that was always kept in a long ponytail. He was always seen wearing a pair of sunglasses. When he was young, he wore a dark kimono with a four-leaf clover pattern; his face was also much rounder compared to its more pointed edges as an adult.<sup id="cite_ref-first_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-first-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> As an adult, he wore a dark kimono with a small crescent moon on the left side of the chest.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Because of his grudge toward Orochi, Denjiro's facial structure changed sometime in the last 20 years. His eyes became slanted, he no longer wears sunglasses, he grew large sideburns, and his hair color lightened considerably. Eventually, he also started hiding his ponytail in a massive faux-pompadour.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> He wears a dark blue kimono with circles and target patterns on it, as well as a blue, high-collared cape.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the raid on <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, he took off his faux-pompadour when revealing his identity.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> When preparing to infiltrate the castle, he wore the Beasts Pirates foot soldier uniform.
</p><p>When going out as Ushimitsu Kozo, Denjiro wore a yellow ninja outfit and put a yellow hokkamuri bandana over his head to hide his hair.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gallery">Gallery</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kyoshiro">Kyoshiro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Denjiro_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest?cb=20211125223309" class="image"><img alt="Denjiro Digitally Colored Manga" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="105" height="105" data-image-name="Denjiro Digitally Colored Manga.png" data-image-key="Denjiro_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Denjiro_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/105?cb=20211125223309" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Denjiro (as Kyoshiro) in the <a href="/wiki/Digitally_Colored_Manga" title="Digitally Colored Manga">Digitally Colored Manga</a>.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Kyoshiro_Anime_Concept_Art.png/revision/latest?cb=20200806203940" class="image"><img alt="Kyoshiro Anime Concept Art" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="63" height="105" data-image-name="Kyoshiro Anime Concept Art.png" data-image-key="Kyoshiro_Anime_Concept_Art.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Kyoshiro_Anime_Concept_Art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/63?cb=20200806203940" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Anime concept art of Denjiro (as Kyoshiro).

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>When he was young, he took pride in his abilities to manipulate people and get what he wants.<sup id="cite_ref-first_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-first-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> He was a fan of <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a> even before becoming his retainer, and held him in high regard for his bold actions.<sup id="cite_ref-c961_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c961-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> After becoming Oden's retainer, he and the rest of the Scabbards worked to aid him in any way, until they were caught by <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</a> during their attempt to steal his money. After being lectured by Yasuie, Denjiro and the rest of the Scabbards became noble and educated samurai. Denjiro, being the more knowledgeable one, was the one who would take some of the teaching onto himself. Denjiro served as the voice of reason for Oden, especially when it came to Kuri's finances. Denjiro attempted to advise Oden against making foolish decisions like giving Orochi money and leaving Wano, though Oden was rarely persuaded.<sup id="cite_ref-c963_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c963-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Oden's death was so traumatic that the very process of grieving caused Denjiro's facial structure to be altered. Denjiro's loyalty and strength of will cannot be understated. An unspecified time after Oden's execution, Denjiro (as <i>Kyoshiro</i>) became a subordinate to <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a> and spent the better part of the past 20 years earning his trust in order to find a chance to overthrow him and restore the Kouzuki Family to power. Denjiro has shown great emotional control, despite his immense hatred for Orochi. He is able to perfectly restrain himself from expressing it and even bowed to the latter as well as protecting him from Zoro in order to not jeopardize the Kouzuki revolution on the Fire Festival.
</p><p>Denjiro has also shown to be very kind, as after becoming Kyoshiro, he works hard in secret to give money to the citizens left impoverished by Orochi's tyranny, and he also took the responsibility of caring for Hiyori after she was separated from Kawamatsu.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As Kyoshiro, Denjiro acts as a cheerful man who loves to drink. While intoxicated, he was unafraid of speaking bluntly about the shogun Orochi despite the potential danger, and he mocked the shogun for believing a prophecy from <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Toki" title="Kouzuki Toki">Kouzuki Toki</a> about his downfall. In this state, he is prone to experiencing rapid mood swings, ranging from laughter to intensity to falling asleep.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> He falls asleep in public frequently due to being up in the middle of the night as Ushimitsu Kozo.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to his self-indulgence, Denjiro does not appear to bother with his obligations as the boss of his <a href="/wiki/Kyoshiro_Family" title="Kyoshiro Family">family</a>. This was seen when he ordered his <a href="/wiki/Kaku_(Wano)" title="Kaku (Wano)">subordinate</a> to contact <a href="/wiki/Queen" title="Queen">Queen</a> himself for an <a href="/wiki/Assassin" title="Assassin">assassin</a> to eliminate an <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">individual</a> who refused to comply with their extortion.<sup id="cite_ref-c927_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c927-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> However, he still cares about his family and will do what he needs to have them defended or avenged, regardless of how low-ranking they are. Ultimately, he is quite diligent when he feels like it, as he was able to raise <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Komurasaki</a> to become <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano</a>'s top-ranking oiran.<sup id="cite_ref-c932_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c932-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> He even protected Orochi as the loyal guard dog from <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>'s attack against the shogun.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> However, his efforts to help Orochi are all a ruse to help the Kouzuki Family on the day of the final battle.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> As Denjiro trapped Sasaki, he showed a confident smile as their revolution proceed smoothly, finally elated that his patience in waiting for a chance to avenge Oden has paid off as he can finally exact revenge on Kaidou and Orochi.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Allies">Allies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="Kin.27emon"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Kin'emon">Kin'emon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Denjiro is one of <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a>'s two oldest and closest friends aside from Tsuru, having known him for years even before they met Kouzuki Oden.<sup id="cite_ref-c960_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c960-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">

  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">If Foxfire Kin'emon and the Nine Red Scabbards should appear... I, for one, would welcome it!! I would enjoy the chance to show you my skill with the blade.</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>

<p>Denjiro eagerly awaits Kin'emon's return for the past 20 years while using his Kyoshiro alias to get close to Orochi in order to find an opportunity to exploit Orochi's trust to his advantage, eventually liberating the imprisoned samurai in the Rasetsu District as well as having his own yakuza family to support Kin'emon in his raid on Onigashima. During the raid, Denjiro revealed himself to his old friend while reminiscing how he had caused the Mountain God Incident, making Kin'emon deeply shocked yet overjoyed as he correctly identified Denjiro as he rejoined the Scabbards.<sup id="cite_ref-c975_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c975-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> He thinks extremely highly of Kin'emon to the point of blind admiration, believing that he cleverly deceived Orochi's <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">spy</a>, when in reality Kin'emon misunderstood Yasuie's message by accident.<sup id="cite_ref-c976_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c976-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Nine_Red_Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20230303041405" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Charge Kaidou" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Scabbards Charge Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230303041405" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20230303041405" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Charge Kaidou" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230303041405" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Scabbards Charge Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230303041405" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Denjiro, alongside the other Red Scabbards (with Izou taking Kanjuro's place), charges into battle.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the past, Denjiro got along with his comrades and worked with them to better serve Oden.
</p><p>Denjiro eagerly awaited their return for the past 20 years, while using his Kyoshiro alias to get close to Orochi in order to find an opportunity to exploit Orochi's trust to his advantage, eventually liberating the imprisoned samurai in the Rasetsu District as well as having his own yakuza family to support Kin'emon in his raid on Onigashima. During the raid, Denjiro revealed himself to his old friends, making them deeply shocked by his new appearance yet overjoyed Denjiro not only rejoined the Scabbards but brought reinforcements.<sup id="cite_ref-c975_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c975-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c976_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c976-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kouzuki_Oden">Kouzuki Oden</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Even before becoming his retainer, Denjiro has immense respect for Oden, believing him to be different from other adults that he considers foolish and that respect increased after witnessing him defeat the Mountain God. Because of his admiration for Oden, Denjiro quickly decided to become his follower after his exile from the Flower Capital.<sup id="cite_ref-c961_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c961-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Although he greatly respected him, Denjiro did sometimes tend to tell Oden off when he kept giving money away to other people so easily, without considering how it would affect their <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">region</a>. In fact, when <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Orochi</a> became the shogun due to Oden's absence, he made it his job to make sure Kuri was well-funded in Oden's stead by borrowing and lending money.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kouzuki_Hiyori">Kouzuki Hiyori</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When he found Hiyori after she was separated from Kawamatsu, he was moved to tears on seeing her alive and well and revealed his true identity to her. After learning about what happened with Kawamatsu, he took on the role as her second protector and raised her using his wealth and resources to groom her to become the highest ranking courtesan.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> He also instructed her to adopt the alias "Komurasaki" to keep herself safe from Orochi and the Beasts Pirates. During Orochi's banquet at the Flower Capital, Hiyori angered the shogun and Denjiro had to fake her death in what looks like a samurai's mercy, which also stopped Orochi from marrying her.<sup id="cite_ref-c933_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c933-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kouzuki_Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As the son of the man whom he served and admired, Denjiro, like the other retainers saw <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</a> as the next shogun and the rightful ruler of Wano, and was determined to help him end the tyrannical reign of Orochi and Kaidou. When he learned of the Beast Pirates attempt to attack Momonosuke and the others at Tokage Port, Denjiro, still in his disguise as Kyoshiro, showed up on his own ship under the pretense of helping the Beast Pirates, only to attack their ships and finally reveal his true identity. Like the other retainers, he was concerned for the young shogun's safety after being taken by Kanjuro, and was prepared to help get him back alongside the other retainers.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kyoshiro_Family">Kyoshiro Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">It doesn't matter how low-ranking some of my underlings are...once we've exchanged sake cups with one another, they're a member of my family!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Denjiro about his subordinates.<sup id="cite_ref-c932_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c932-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
As the boss of the <a href="/wiki/Kyoshiro_Family" title="Kyoshiro Family">Kyoshiro Family</a>, he appears to care greatly about his subordinates, having performed a <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki_(Ceremony)" title="Sakazuki (Ceremony)">sakazuki ceremony</a> with them. Thus, if any of them are wronged, he will take the necessary steps to target those who wronged them.<sup id="cite_ref-c932_14-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c932-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> He will not interfere with his own plans to help his subordinates in this regard, but he still ensures they are helped by telling them to contact the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c927_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c927-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> It seems that his followers are loyal enough to join him in becoming enemies of Orochi and the Beasts Pirates.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kurozumi_Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Denjiro_Bowing_to_Orochi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220608020034" class="image"><img alt="Denjiro Bowing to Orochi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Denjiro Bowing to Orochi.png" data-image-key="Denjiro_Bowing_to_Orochi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Denjiro_Bowing_to_Orochi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220608020034" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Denjiro_Bowing_to_Orochi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220608020034" class="image"><img alt="Denjiro Bowing to Orochi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Denjiro_Bowing_to_Orochi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220608020034" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Denjiro Bowing to Orochi.png" data-image-key="Denjiro_Bowing_to_Orochi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Denjiro_Bowing_to_Orochi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220608020034" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Denjiro_Bowing_to_Orochi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Denjiro bowing to Orochi while being internally furious.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Due to Orochi being one of the two masterminds behind Oden's death, Denjiro held immense rage and hatred for <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Orochi</a>. Thus, he feigned unwavering loyalty and allegiance towards the latter, having diligently worked for 20 years to gain his trust until the right time comes to overthrow him and restore the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a> to power.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> He also denied Orochi's chance to marry Komurasaki (in actuality Hiyori) by faking her death.<sup id="cite_ref-c974_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c974-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While in Orochi's presence under his Kyoshiro persona, Denjiro acted submissive and with extreme reverence, being inclined to spout phrases and ideas that the shogun would agree with, and Orochi complimented Kyoshiro when he voiced these ideas.<sup id="cite_ref-c932_14-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c932-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> He even referred to himself as the shogun's "lap dog".<sup id="cite_ref-c944_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Unlike most of Orochi's associates, Denjiro acted derisive of the shogun's paranoia over the return of the Kouzuki Family and openly mocked Orochi as a coward while intoxicated on <a href="/wiki/Foods/Beverages#Alcohol" title="Foods/Beverages">alcohol</a>, albeit not within Orochi's earshot.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In reality, Denjiro also agreed with Orochi's beliefs in the comeback of the Kouzuki Family as Denjiro fully intended to betray Orochi by eventually rejoining the Nine Red Scabbards to avenge Oden's death which he did by using the authority Orochi gave him to liberate the one thousand Kouzuki samurai loyalists imprisoned in the Rasetsu district to join Kin'emon in the raid on Onigashima. As the revolution proceeded smoothly, Denjiro gave a sinister smile at finally making Orochi pay for what he did to Oden and the Wano citizens. When Orochi realizes who Kyoshiro really is, he praises Denjiro for his deception skill. He was even able to cut off one of Orochi's heads alongside the other samurai.<sup id="cite_ref-c1009_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1009-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Denjiro ultimately ended Orochi's life by decapitating his final head.<sup id="cite_ref-c1048_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1048-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kurozumi_Kanjuro">Kurozumi Kanjuro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In the past, they were well acquainted and served Oden faithfully.
</p><p>During the raid, Denjiro became aware of Kanjuro being the spy but believed he was deceived by Kin'emon.<sup id="cite_ref-c976_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c976-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Beast_Pirates">Beast Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In his guise as Kyoshiro, Denjiro deceived the crew into trusting him and like his subordinates, they refer to him as "Boss". During the raid, they were relieved to see him appear when dealing with their enemies. Denjiro then revealed his true allegiance by destroying one of the Beasts Pirates' ships and joining his true allies.<sup id="cite_ref-c976_17-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c976-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Denjiro aided his allies in attacking Kaidou, who was surprised to learn that Kyoshiro is actually Denjiro. When the Scabbards actually injured Kaidou that made him scream in pain, he went serious enough to take the battle outside of the Skull Dome with the Scabbards.<sup id="cite_ref-c987_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c987-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>As a member of the Nine Red Scabbards, Denjiro is a powerful samurai whom <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a> states (alongside <a href="/wiki/Kawamatsu" title="Kawamatsu">Kawamatsu</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ashura_Doji" title="Ashura Doji">Ashura Doji</a>) is worth 100 men in battle.<sup id="cite_ref-c921_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c921-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> By combining his power with that of three other Scabbards, he was able to seriously injure the former <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a> <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> in his full dragon form.<sup id="cite_ref-Togen_Totsuka_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Togen_Totsuka-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As the boss of the <a href="/wiki/Kyoshiro_Family" title="Kyoshiro Family">Kyoshiro Family</a> and (formerly) one of the highest-ranking subordinates of the <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Family" title="Kurozumi Family">Kurozumi Family</a>, Denjiro is one of the wealthiest, most influential citizens of the Flower Capital, able to hire high-ranking geisha dancers to perform for him.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> He had enough wealth to sponsor and groom Hiyori into the highest-ranking oiran in Wano. As a yakuza boss, Denjiro commands strong henchmen who can extort businesses for <a href="/wiki/Belly#Other_Currencies" title="Belly">money</a>. Thanks to his connections with <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano</a>'s shogunate, Denjiro could strengthen his group further by requesting assistance from his allies, notably the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c927_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c927-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> who appeared to treat him quite respectfully before his betrayal was revealed, as <a href="/wiki/Page_One" title="Page One">Page One</a> referred to him as "Boss Kyoshiro"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">狂死郎親分</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kyōshirō Oyabun</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Denjiro possesses immense physical strength, being able to clash with <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a> in terms of physical power.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_15-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c945_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c945-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> When he first walked into the Flower Capital as Kyoshiro, he easily beat aside two men who confronted him, and his display of strength impressed other men into wanting to become his followers.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Alongside his fellow Scabbards, Denjiro managed to push <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> off his feet when ambushing him.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> He was capable of effortlessly decapitating Kurozumi Orochi, in his massive Mythical Zoan form, with the shogun being unable to react either time.<sup id="cite_ref-c1009_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1009-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1048_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1048-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Denjiro is extremely agile, as shown when he ran and leapt across rooftops when robbing houses at night as Ushimitsu Kozo.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Intelligence">Intelligence</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From a very young age, Denjiro was extremely clever and persuasive, a skill he would use to trick and swindle other people, including shopkeepers, for his own gain. He also showed extensive knowledge regarding the politics of the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Flower Capital</a> yakuza.<sup id="cite_ref-c960_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c960-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> He also learned faster than his fellow Nine Red Scabbards during their self-education, later teaching them himself. 
</p><p>During his years as Kyoshiro, Denjiro showed great cunning, having not only founded his own yakuza family but also was quickly able to get into Orochi's service, becoming one of his highest ranking subordinates and gaining enough influence to have connections with the Beasts Pirates while perfectly hiding his allegiances to the Kouzuki Family. He was able to earn the trust of the extremely cunning and cautious Orochi to be placed in charge of the Flower Capital during the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Festival" title="Fire Festival">Fire Festival</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Denjiro is a masterful thief both because of his charisma as well as his ability to sneak into other people's homes and steal money. For at least thirteen years, he has robbed homes in the Flower Capital at night without anyone realizing his identity.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Orochi fell in love with Komurasaki, Denjiro devised a clever idea to separate the two of them, telling Hiyori to carry a blood bag so he could fake her death when necessary. After years of servitude towards Orochi, Denjiro was able to gain insight into Orochi's mindset, correctly deducing the fact he had implanted a spy among his comrades, which Orochi had kept secret from most people except Kaidou. Thus, Denjiro had opted to reveal his identity to Kin'emon only during the Fire Festival.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tactical_Skills">Tactical Skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Denjiro's intellect makes him an outstanding tactician. He chose to take full advantage of his changed appearance to live under a different identity, putting on a front of submitting to Orochi and becoming one of his most loyal subordinates in order to amass both wealth and influence that allowed him to further his cause in supporting the Kouzuki Family such as raising and protecting Kouzuki Hiyori for thirteen years. 
</p><p>He showed incredible caution, as he advised Hiyori to live under an alias to protect herself from Orochi and the Beasts Pirates, and came up with a plan of faking her death that allowed her to escape Orochi's wrath. He also instructed Hiyori to keep his identity a secret from even their allies, which would prove crucial as Kanjuro, a fellow member of the Nine Red Scabbards, was revealed to be a spy for Orochi. 
</p><p>Denjiro was opportunistic enough to exploit the trust of Orochi and the Beast Pirates, using his temporary authority over the Flower Capital to liberate the one thousand prisoners of Rasetsu District to join him in the Kouzuki revolution as well as sinking one of the Beasts Pirates' ships when they let their guard down in his presence. Denjiro would also repeat this deception on Sasaki, one of the Beast Pirates' Tobiroppo who still thought he was an ally, with Denjiro being able to subdue him without any effort.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Swordsmanship">Swordsmanship</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Oden_Two_Sword_Style" title="Oden Two Sword Style">Oden Two Sword Style</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest?cb=20220621131809" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Use Oden Two Sword Style" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Scabbards Use Oden Two Sword Style.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20220621131809" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest?cb=20220621131809" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Use Oden Two Sword Style" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20220621131809" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Scabbards Use Oden Two Sword Style.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20220621131809" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Denjiro, alongside three other Scabbards, wields Oden Two Sword Style against Kaidou.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Denjiro possesses the greatest mastery in swordsmanship among the Nine Red Scabbards.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> His skill was shown when he deflected Roronoa Zoro's <i>720-Pound Phoenix</i> with ease and proceeded to evenly clash with Zoro's Two Sword Style with only one sword for a brief time, preventing him from pursuing Orochi.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_15-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> He was masterful enough to precisely cut through the blood bag Hiyori wore under her kimono without striking her body, allowing them to fake her death while she remained unharmed in reality.<sup id="cite_ref-c933_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c933-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c974_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c974-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> He cleanly cut through one of the Beasts Pirates' massive ships with a flying slash.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Denjiro is also capable of emulating Oden's signature <b>Oden Two Sword Style</b> style, allowing him to fight wielding two swords and perform one of his techniques.<sup id="cite_ref-Togen_Totsuka_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Togen_Totsuka-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Denjiro is a master of <a href="/wiki/Armament_Haki" class="mw-redirect" title="Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>, which is known as "Ryuo" in Wano. He can harden his swords and possesses an advanced level of Armament Haki, as shown when he cuts through Kaidou's tremendously tough skin.<sup id="cite_ref-Togen_Totsuka_26-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Togen_Totsuka-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the anime when Denjiro uses advanced Armament Haki, it is shown as a yellow and orange colored flowing aura.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Denjiro possesses the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Observation_Haki" class="mw-redirect" title="Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Retainer_of_the_Kouzuki_Family">Retainer of the Kouzuki Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Denjiro was an orphan living in the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Flower Capital</a>. At one time 41 years ago, he swindled a pot merchant.<sup id="cite_ref-first_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-first-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> He met up with <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a>, who showed him a <a href="/wiki/Koyama" title="Koyama">white boar</a>. Denjiro then informed Kin'emon that the boar was an offspring of the <a href="/wiki/Mountain_God" title="Mountain God">Mountain God</a>, which began attacking the capital. The two were approached by <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>, who asked them to give the boar to him.<sup id="cite_ref-c960_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c960-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Kin%27emon_and_Denjiro_Serving_Oden.png/revision/latest?cb=20210207040644" class="image"><img alt="Kin&#39;emon and Denjiro Serving Oden" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kin&#39;emon and Denjiro Serving Oden.png" data-image-key="Kin%27emon_and_Denjiro_Serving_Oden.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Kin%27emon_and_Denjiro_Serving_Oden.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210207040644" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Kin%27emon_and_Denjiro_Serving_Oden.png/revision/latest?cb=20210207040644" class="image"><img alt="Kin&#39;emon and Denjiro Serving Oden" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Kin%27emon_and_Denjiro_Serving_Oden.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210207040644" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kin&#39;emon and Denjiro Serving Oden.png" data-image-key="Kin%27emon_and_Denjiro_Serving_Oden.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Kin%27emon_and_Denjiro_Serving_Oden.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210207040644" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kin%27emon_and_Denjiro_Serving_Oden.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Denjiro and Kin'emon begin to serve Oden.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Oden tried to take the boar from Kin'emon, Denjiro expressed his admiration for Oden. He then panicked when Kin'emon tried to attack the Mountain God but was awestruck to witness Oden <a href="/wiki/Mountain_God_Incident" title="Mountain God Incident">striking down the beast</a>. As Oden left the capital in exile, Denjiro decided to become his follower. He and Kin'emon then followed Oden to <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</a>'s residence at <a href="/wiki/Hakumai" title="Hakumai">Hakumai</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c961_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c961-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> They later followed Oden on his journey to <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">Kuri</a>. After Oden became daimyo of Kuri, Denjiro became one of his retainers.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kawamatsu" title="Kawamatsu">Kawamatsu</a> joined Oden, they were running low on funds. Therefore, he and the other retainers attempted to steal money from Yasuie, but they were caught. Instead of punishing them, Yasuie allowed them to take the money and encouraged them to use it to become better people for the sake of Oden and <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>. Following Yasuie's advice, they educated themselves and trained to become dignified warriors. 30 years ago, they visited the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Flower Capital</a> with Oden.<sup id="cite_ref-c963_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c963-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After meeting the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a>, Oden and his retainers were having a feast with them. Oden said that he wanted to join the crew, but Denjiro, <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">Kanjuro</a>, Kin'emon, and <a href="/wiki/Raizo" title="Raizo">Raizo</a> voiced out against it. After the Whitebeard Pirates left Wano two weeks later, the retainers discovered Oden, <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">Izou</a>, Inuarashi, and Nekomamushi to be missing.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While Oden was away, Denjiro went all over Wano, borrowing money.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Oden failed to kill <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a> 25 years ago, the retainers remained loyal to him for the next five years despite Oden acting like a fool and losing the respect of most of Wano's people. 20 years ago, Oden finally had enough and decided to take down Kaidou. The retainers eagerly followed him and marched with him to <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On the way to Onigashima, the group was confronted by <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> and <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">his crew</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Udon" title="Udon">Udon</a> region. <a href="/wiki/Shinobu" title="Shinobu">Shinobu</a> joined the <a href="/wiki/Samurai" title="Samurai">samurai</a> and in the ensuing battle, Denjiro and Kanjuro fought <a href="/wiki/Queen" title="Queen">Queen</a>. Unfortunately, the samurai were overwhelmed in the end. Oden and the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a> were then imprisoned in the Flower Capital and sentenced to be boiled alive in three days.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png/revision/latest?cb=20191208071646" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou vs Red Scabbards" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="112" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kaidou vs Red Scabbards.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20191208071646" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png/revision/latest?cb=20191208071646" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou vs Red Scabbards" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20191208071646" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="112" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kaidou vs Red Scabbards.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20191208071646" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Denjiro and Ashura facing Kaidou.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>All ten prisoners were later brought to the execution site, at which point Oden made a deal with Kaidou. After Oden stepped into the pot of boiling oil, the retainers were about to join him, but Oden grabbed a plank and ordered them to stand on it as he held them over the pot.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> As Oden endured <a href="/wiki/Legendary_Hour" title="Legendary Hour">the hour</a>, he explained to his retainers the reason Wano Country was isolated and requested them to open Wano's borders for him. Oden successfully survived the hour, but Orochi summoned a firing squad to execute Oden and his retainers. Oden once again told his retainers to open Wano's borders before throwing them far away from the pot. The Scabbards fled with tears as Oden met his demise.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> With an army of pursuers chasing them, Denjiro and <a href="/wiki/Ashura_Doji" title="Ashura Doji">Ashura Doji</a> split from the group to fight their enemies.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> At some point, Denjiro and Ashura battled Kaidou together.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Becoming_Kyoshiro">Becoming Kyoshiro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e2/Denjiro_Transformed.png/revision/latest?cb=20210602061909" class="image"><img alt="Denjiro Transformed" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Denjiro Transformed.png" data-image-key="Denjiro_Transformed.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e2/Denjiro_Transformed.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210602061909" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e2/Denjiro_Transformed.png/revision/latest?cb=20210602061909" class="image"><img alt="Denjiro Transformed" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e2/Denjiro_Transformed.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210602061909" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Denjiro Transformed.png" data-image-key="Denjiro_Transformed.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e2/Denjiro_Transformed.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210602061909" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Denjiro_Transformed.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Denjiro's rage transforms his face.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Denjiro escaped and went to an abandoned shrine atop a hill, where he was consumed by rage over Oden's death for a long period of time. His rage was so severe that by the time Denjiro emerged from the hut, not only had he destroyed his glasses, but his hair had changed color and his face had become so twisted it was unrecognisable.
