He came to the Flower Capital, where he was confronted over his rough appearance. Denjiro quickly beat his foes to the ground, resulting in other men wanting to become his followers. When they asked for his name, Denjiro called himself Kyoshiro.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Denjiro gathered a large number of followers, and with his newfound power, he offered to serve Orochi as his bodyguard and supply the shogun with more riches. Orochi agreed, and Denjiro thus rose to power as the top <a href="/wiki/Yakuza" title="Yakuza">yakuza</a> boss, with him and his followers becoming known as the <a href="/wiki/Kyoshiro_Family" title="Kyoshiro Family">Kyoshiro Family</a>. At night, Denjiro would disguise himself and steal from the homes of rich Flower Capital citizens and give the money to impoverished villages outside the capital. The people who spotted him committing these robberies would call him Ushimitsu Kozo. Seven years after Oden's death, <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Kouzuki Hiyori</a> was brought outside Denjiro's residence after being found on the streets of the Flower Capital. Denjiro brought Hiyori in and revealed his true identity to her.<sup id="cite_ref-c973_2-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c973-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> He then raised her for the next 13 years and made her into an oiran named Komurasaki. Denjiro was seen with Hiyori as an adult when she swindled a man named <a href="/wiki/Bingo" title="Bingo">Bingo</a> of all his money. Due to Orochi falling in love with Komurasaki, Denjiro advised Hiyori to carry fake blood under her kimono so he could fake her death if the situation requires it.<sup id="cite_ref-c974_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c974-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Arc">Wano Country Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As he was drinking alcohol, Denjiro began to mock <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a> for living in fear of the prophecy stated by Oden's wife <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Toki" title="Kouzuki Toki">Toki</a>, which was that the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a> would avenge themselves after 20 years. They were now at the 20th year, and Denjiro stated that he could not believe that this would happen since the entire family had supposedly died.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After he was invited to Orochi's banquet, Denjiro heard from a subordinate that a <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">soba shop owner</a> beat up some of his henchmen. Since he would be attending the banquet, he ordered the subordinate to contact <a href="/wiki/Queen" title="Queen">Queen</a> to send <a href="/wiki/Assassin" title="Assassin">assassins</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c927_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c927-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> He later went to the banquet hall at <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital#Orochi_Castle" title="Flower Capital">Orochi's palace</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While at the banquet, Denjiro was praised for raising Komurasaki, whom Orochi was courting, as well as for his response to the attack on his subordinates. Orochi commended Denjiro's use of excessive force and took the opportunity to talk about Toki's prophecy. Komurasaki's kamuro <a href="/wiki/Toko" title="Toko">Toko</a> ended up laughing at Orochi, and chaos started breaking out as an altercation between the three of them started. Denjiro pulled out his <a href="/wiki/Sword" title="Sword">sword</a>, saying a bloodbath was about to occur.<sup id="cite_ref-c932_14-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c932-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/57/Kyoshiro_Attacks_Komurasaki.png/revision/latest?cb=20230302162731" class="image"><img alt="Kyoshiro Attacks Komurasaki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kyoshiro Attacks Komurasaki.png" data-image-key="Kyoshiro_Attacks_Komurasaki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/57/Kyoshiro_Attacks_Komurasaki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230302162731" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/57/Kyoshiro_Attacks_Komurasaki.png/revision/latest?cb=20230302162731" class="image"><img alt="Kyoshiro Attacks Komurasaki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/57/Kyoshiro_Attacks_Komurasaki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230302162731" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kyoshiro Attacks Komurasaki.png" data-image-key="Kyoshiro_Attacks_Komurasaki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/57/Kyoshiro_Attacks_Komurasaki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230302162731" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kyoshiro_Attacks_Komurasaki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Denjiro seemingly strikes down "Komurasaki".</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Orochi went berserk in his <a href="/wiki/Hebi_Hebi_no_Mi,_Model:_Yamata_no_Orochi" title="Hebi Hebi no Mi, Model: Yamata no Orochi">multi-headed dragon</a> form and one of his heads grabbed Komurasaki. When she ended up being freed from his grasp, Denjiro slashed her with the appearance of killing her. Believing Komurasaki to be dead, Orochi was shocked and furious at his actions, but Denjiro reminded him of her crime. He then found a card containing <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a>'s secret message.<sup id="cite_ref-c933_19-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c933-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Denjiro returned to the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital#Red-Light_District" title="Flower Capital">Red-Light District</a> and was informed that Komurasaki's wake was cancelled. One of <a href="/wiki/Kyoshiro_Family" title="Kyoshiro Family">Denjiro's cohorts</a> warned him about those who bear a grudge against him, but Denjiro bluntly replied that there was nothing else he could have done and he had already suffered the biggest loss from Komurasaki's "death". Denjiro also stated that Orochi was very enraged because of Kin'emon's secret message card.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He later returned to the palace. After Orochi was informed of the capture of <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Yasuie</a>, Denjiro explained that the <a href="/wiki/Animal_Species/Wano_Country_Saga#Picture_Tanishi" title="Animal Species/Wano Country Saga">Picture Tanishi</a> was prepared.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> At <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital#Rasetsu_Town" title="Flower Capital">Rasetsu Town</a>, when <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a> attempted to attack Orochi with an <a href="/wiki/Three_Sword_Style/Two_Sword_Style#After_the_Timeskip" title="Three Sword Style/Two Sword Style">air slash</a>, Denjiro blocked the attack before engaging Zoro in battle.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_15-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> His clash with Zoro was interrupted when one of the <a href="/wiki/Orochi_Oniwabanshu" title="Orochi Oniwabanshu">Orochi Oniwabanshu</a> intervened.<sup id="cite_ref-c945_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c945-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On the day of the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Festival" title="Fire Festival">Fire Festival</a>, Denjiro was left in charge of the Flower Capital while Orochi departed for <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, Denjiro freed the 1,000 samurai that were imprisoned in Rasetsu Town, and together with the Kyoshiro Family, they went to where the confrontation between the Beasts Pirates and the samurai alliance was. There, Denjiro attacked one of the Beasts Pirates ships, revealed his true identity as Denjiro, and he then revealed that <a href="/wiki/Yasuie" class="mw-redirect" title="Yasuie">Yasuie</a>'s altered message actually instructed the Kouzuki allies to meet at the wharf by Habu Port. Thus, their allies had been able to reach the wharf before Orochi destroyed the bridges. As he revealed this, the alliance, now numbering 5400, arrived at Tokage Port on a massive fleet. Denjiro commended <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a> for cleverly misinforming the other Scabbards to mislead the spy Kanjuro, unaware that Kin'emon had actually misunderstood the message.<sup id="cite_ref-c975_8-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c975-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kanjuro then fled the scene with Momonosuke in tow on a <a href="/wiki/Fude_Fude_no_Mi" title="Fude Fude no Mi">drawn crane</a> and briefly attacked the alliance with an ink cloud that rained down ink arrows. Momonosuke ordered the alliance to press forward to Onigashima without worrying about him. As the alliance was attacked by a Beasts Pirates ship with long ranged cannons, <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> came to aid the rebels.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After <a href="/wiki/Shishilian" title="Shishilian">Shishilian</a> and Hyogoro boarded the <a href="/wiki/Polar_Tang" title="Polar Tang">Polar Tang</a>, the Scabbards discussed with <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Law</a> about the plan to enter Onigashima. Denjiro was then surprised to see the Straw Hats take over the port in front of Onigashima.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> While the rest of the Scabbards traversed to the back of Onigashima with the <a href="/wiki/Heart_Pirates" title="Heart Pirates">Heart Pirates</a> in Law's submarine, Denjiro and Kin'emon entered Onigashima through the front with the rest of the alliance.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After receiving <a href="/wiki/Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi" title="Fuku Fuku no Mi">Beasts Pirates disguises</a>, the alliance divided their forces with Denjiro leading the southern forces.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> On the way to their destination, Denjiro's group came across a gate and Denjiro discarded his Beasts Pirates disguise. He encountered <a href="/wiki/Sasaki" title="Sasaki">Sasaki</a>, who still thought he was one of Orochi's allies. With Sasaki's guard down, Denjiro had him shackled.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20231121020441" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Attack Kaidou" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="216" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Scabbards Attack Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20231121020441" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20231121020441" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Attack Kaidou" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20231121020441" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="216" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Scabbards Attack Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20231121020441" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Scabbards and Izou attack Kaidou.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Denjiro and Kin'emon later joined up with the other Scabbards and Izou at the back entrance and found Kanjuro laying on the ground defeated. They then entered Kaidou's castle, fought their way to the Performance Stage, and launched an all-out attack on Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> While falling to the lower floor, the Scabbards managed to inflict wounds on Kaidou. As the alliance revealed themselves and attacked the Beasts Pirates, Kaidou transformed into <a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">his dragon form</a> and flew to the roof of the <a href="/wiki/Skull_Dome" title="Skull Dome">Skull Dome</a>, with the Scabbards grabbing onto him. On the roof, the Scabbards prepared to fight Kaidou with the <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">Mink Tribe</a>'s help.<sup id="cite_ref-c987_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c987-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png/revision/latest?cb=20230313024406" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Strike Kaidou&#39;s Scar" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Scabbards Strike Kaidou&#39;s Scar.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230313024406" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png/revision/latest?cb=20230313024406" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Strike Kaidou&#39;s Scar" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230313024406" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Scabbards Strike Kaidou&#39;s Scar.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230313024406" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Denjiro and three other Scabbards slash Kaidou's scar.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a> and a platoon arrived at the roof, the Scabbards watched as the <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a> minks engaged the enemy.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> After Jack and his forces were defeated, the Scabbards resumed their confrontation with Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Kaidou roared lightning at them, but they dodged around it and each struck him in turn. After Raizo reflected Kaidou's Bolo Breath back at him, four of the Scabbards—Denjiro, Ashura, Kin'emon, and Inuarashi—replicated <a href="/wiki/Oden_Two_Sword_Style" title="Oden Two Sword Style">Oden's Two Sword Style</a> stance and struck Kaidou's scar with the same attack that made it.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Kaidou then retaliated with a roar that created wind scythes aimed at the Scabbards.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> After returning to human form, Kaidou began overwhelming the Scabbards<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> and later incapacitated them.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eustass_Kid" title="Eustass Kid">Eustass Kid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Killer" title="Killer">Killer</a>, Zoro, <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>, and Law later arrived at the roof. Upon Luffy's request, Law <a href="/wiki/Ope_Ope_no_Mi" title="Ope Ope no Mi">teleported</a> the Scabbards to a safe place.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> They were placed in the treasure room on the second floor, where a mysterious person was tending to them.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> The Scabbards later recovered and regained consciousness, but the mysterious figure already had left. Before they left the treasure room, they saw who appeared to be Oden.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> After Ashura revealed it to be a fake, Denjiro realized that it was the work of Kanjuro and began fighting it. When the fake Oden attempted to blow itself up alongside the Scabbards, Ashura sacrificed himself to push the fake out of the building, saving the others. They then headed out in pursuit of Kanjuro and Momonosuke.
</p><p>After Inuarashi remained behind to fight Jack,<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> the rest encounter Orochi and <a href="/wiki/Fukurokuju" title="Fukurokuju">Fukurokuju</a>, who were setting fires around the castle. Orochi mocked them and then transformed to attack them, but they severed his heads and left, believing him dead. Raizo then stayed behind to fight Fukurokuju.<sup id="cite_ref-c1009_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1009-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Along the way, Denjiro split off from the group.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Denjiro_Beheads_Orochi.png/revision/latest?cb=20230910021802" class="image"><img alt="Denjiro Beheads Orochi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="182" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Denjiro Beheads Orochi.png" data-image-key="Denjiro_Beheads_Orochi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Denjiro_Beheads_Orochi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230910021802" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Denjiro_Beheads_Orochi.png/revision/latest?cb=20230910021802" class="image"><img alt="Denjiro Beheads Orochi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Denjiro_Beheads_Orochi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230910021802" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="182" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Denjiro Beheads Orochi.png" data-image-key="Denjiro_Beheads_Orochi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Denjiro_Beheads_Orochi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230910021802" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Denjiro_Beheads_Orochi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Denjiro beheads Orochi.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Denjiro later returned to the Treasure Repository, where Orochi was attacking Hiyori. Denjiro beheaded Orochi again and protectively hugged Hiyori.<sup id="cite_ref-c1048_23-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1048-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Denjiro then praised her for remaining strong all these years.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Suddenly, however, Orochi was still alive, who continued to threaten Hiyori. Despite Denjiro telling her to be careful, Hiyori approached Orochi to convey her answer, who after listening to her finally died from the fire.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Afterwards, Nekomamushi announced that Luffy had defeated Kaidou and that Momonosuke had safely landed the island. After Momonosuke announces to all the citizens of the Flower Capital that Kaido's rule has ended, the Scabbards accompany Hiyori to calm the panicking citizens. When they see him, they ask about his new hairstyle, to which Denjiro replies that it is a long story, where he announces to them about the new shogun.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> As the citizens marveled at the return of the Nine Red Scabbards, they broadcast this to the entire country. There, the Scabbards kneel before Momonosuke, when he appears in his human form. After Momonosuke broadcast his speech to the entire country and the new shogun was proclaimed, Denjiro started crying. To then enter the shogun's castle with the others.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png/revision/latest?cb=20231029020649" class="image"><img alt="Aramaki vs the Scabbards" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Aramaki vs the Scabbards.png" data-image-key="Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231029020649" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png/revision/latest?cb=20231029020649" class="image"><img alt="Aramaki vs the Scabbards" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231029020649" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Aramaki vs the Scabbards.png" data-image-key="Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231029020649" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Aramaki_vs_the_Scabbards.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The samurai ready to protect Luffy from Ryokugyu.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A week later, Denjiro was enjoying the ongoing festivities when Luffy, who had finally woken up, raised a toast for the Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance and Wano citizens.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> When the Kouzuki Retainers noticed <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Aramaki" title="Aramaki">Ryokugyu</a>'s approach, several of them, including Denjiro, went out to stop him from entering the Flower Capital. Using <a href="/wiki/Mori_Mori_no_Mi" title="Mori Mori no Mi">his Devil Fruit powers</a>, Ryokugyu attacked the samurai and announced his intent to go after Luffy. They were joined by Yamato and Momonosuke, and the retainers became distressed as Ryokugyu restrained the shogun.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> When Momonosuke managed to free them with a Bolo Breath that destroyed the admiral's plant body, Denjiro was impressed. However, despite Momonosuke attacking him again with the same attack, Ryogukyu rebuilt himself again. Just as they were about to be attacked by the admiral again, <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> from outside Wano forced Ryogukyu to leave the country.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png/revision/latest?cb=20231126020849" class="image"><img alt="Momonosuke as the Shogun" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Momonosuke as the Shogun.png" data-image-key="Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231126020849" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png/revision/latest?cb=20231126020849" class="image"><img alt="Momonosuke as the Shogun" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231126020849" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Momonosuke as the Shogun.png" data-image-key="Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231126020849" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Momonosuke_as_the_Shogun.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Denjiro with his fellow samurai ready to serve their Shogun.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, along with some of his fellow Scabbards, he was present when Tenguyama reveals that he is actually <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Sukiyaki" title="Kouzuki Sukiyaki">Kouzuki Sukiyaki</a>. However, all the servants (except Kin'emon) confirm that they already knew his identity before. Sukiyaki asks them not to reveal his identity to anyone, saying that he wants them to forge the new age, to which they agreed. Days later, Denjiro and the others (except Kin'emon and Momonosuke) said goodbye to the Straw Hats in the morning. <sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Denjiro later accompanied the others to the Flower Capital with Momonosuke as the new shogun was look a place to hang the Straw Hats' <a href="/wiki/Jolly_Roger" title="Jolly Roger">Jolly Roger</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="Oni_Child_Yamato.27s_Golden_Harvest_Surrogate_Pilgrimage"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Oni_Child_Yamato's_Golden_Harvest_Surrogate_Pilgrimage">Oni Child Yamato's Golden Harvest Surrogate Pilgrimage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When Yamato was being bullied by children in <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country#Kibi" title="Wano Country">Kibi</a>, Denjiro, now the new <a href="/wiki/Daimyo" title="Daimyo">daimyo</a> of Kibi, went and put a stop to it by placing them inside a net.<sup id="cite_ref-c1120_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1120-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> He punished the kids, though it turned out to actually be eating oden with Yamato, which they all enjoyed.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Playable_Appearances">Playable Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FDenjiro%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 100px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/51/Volume_Change_725a.png/revision/latest?cb=20150613015020" class="image"><img alt="Volume Change 725a" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="100" height="222" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Volume Change 725a.png" data-image-key="Volume_Change_725a.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/51/Volume_Change_725a.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20150613015020" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/51/Volume_Change_725a.png/revision/latest?cb=20150613015020" class="image"><img alt="Volume Change 725a" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/51/Volume_Change_725a.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20150613015020" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="100" height="222" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Volume Change 725a.png" data-image-key="Volume_Change_725a.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/51/Volume_Change_725a.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20150613015020" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Volume_Change_725a.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kanjuro's former silhouette.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Denjiro's design resembles the initial silhouette of <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">Kanjuro</a> that was shown in the magazine release of <a href="/wiki/Chapter_725" title="Chapter 725">Chapter 725</a>.</li>
<li>Denjiro being Kyoshiro was first hinted at in the anime opening <a href="/wiki/OVER_THE_TOP" title="OVER THE TOP">OVER THE TOP</a>, in which he was shown in a shot with <a href="/wiki/Ashura_Doji" title="Ashura Doji">Ashura Doji</a> in a shot montage of the Nine Red Scabbards. The opening debuted eight months before Kyoshiro was revealed to be Denjiro in the manga.</li>
<li>Denjiro's guise identity is most likely named after <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nemuri_Ky%C5%8Dshir%C5%8D" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nemuri Kyōshirō">Nemuri Kyōshirō</a>, a series of novels written by Renzaburo Shibata, whose title character is a sleepy-eyed ronin in the Edo period.</li>
<li>Ushimitsu Kozo is very likely based off of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nezumi_Koz%C5%8D" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nezumi Kozō">Nezumi Kozō</a>, a Japanese thief. After he was executed, he was made into a folk hero who stole from the rich and gave to the poor, like the English legendary bandit <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robin_Hood" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robin Hood">Robin Hood</a>. <i>Nezumi Kozō</i> is a nickname meaning "rat boy", just as <i>Ushimitsu Kozō</i> means "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Witching_hour_(supernatural)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Witching hour (supernatural)">witching hour</a> boy".</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a> claimed that she was Ushimitsu Kozo when confronted by the <a href="/wiki/Orochi_Oniwabanshu" title="Orochi Oniwabanshu">Orochi Oniwabanshu</a>, but <a href="/wiki/Fukurokuju" title="Fukurokuju">Fukurokuju</a> exposed her lie immediately because the timing was not correct.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</a> impersonated Ushimitsu Kozo in order to be given a public execution, allowing him to use his platform to deceive Orochi's forces. When he revealed that him being Ushimitsu Kozo was a lie, the guards realized that they caught him stealing from the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Flower Capital</a> an hour before Ushimitsu Kozo actually committed thefts.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Denjiro's favorite food is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tendon_as_food" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tendon as food">beef tendon</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-sbs96_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs96-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> and his least favorite food is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Char-grilled_steak" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Char-grilled steak">char-grilled</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kusaya" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kusaya">kusaya</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
<ul><li>Fittingly enough, beef tendon is one of the main ingredients in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Oden">oden</a>, just as Denjiro was one of <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden's</a> main retainers.</li></ul></li>
<li>Denjiro's animal resemblance is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Borzoi" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Borzoi">borzoi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Denjiro's hobby is taking <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Siesta" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Siesta">siestas</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> a reference his epithet "Dozing Kyoshiro".</li></ul>
